	}

	# ai importance placed on this CB: scope is the targeted title, ROOT is the attacking character, FROM is the defending character
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1.25 #Use before single claim wars
		#Dragon intimidation
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			ROOT = {
				NOT = { can_use_dragon_abilities_trigger = yes }
				NOT = { relative_power = { who = FROM power = 6 } }
			}
			FROM = {
				can_use_dragon_abilities_trigger = yes
				OR = {
					any_friend = { trait = dragon martial = 60 }
					AND = {  graphical_culture = dragongfx martial = 60 }
				}
				is_incapable = no
			}
		}
		modifier = { #Should prefer Bloody Vengeance if possible
			factor = 0.1
			ROOT = {
				OR = {
					has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_vengeance }
					has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_blood_feud }
					has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_burned_closed_relative }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}


change_seniority_succession_law = {
	name = CB_NAME_SENIORITY_SUCCESSION_LAW
	war_name = WAR_NAME_SENIORITY_SUCCESSION_LAW
	sprite = 6
	truce_days = 3650
	attacker_can_call_allies = no
	can_ask_to_join_war = no
	#major_revolt = yes

	infamy_modifier = 0

	can_use = {
		ROOT = {
			vassal_of = FROM
		}
	}

	is_valid = {
	}

	is_valid_title = {
		NOT = {
			has_law = succ_seniority
		}
		OR = {
			tier = emperor
			tier = king
			is_primary_holder_title = yes
		}
	}

	on_success = {
		hidden_tooltip = {
			ROOT = { add_character_modifier = { name = victory_timer duration = 3 } }
			mega_war_rebel_leader_resolution_effect = yes
		}
		FROM = {
			hidden_tooltip = { disband_event_forces = faction_loyalists }
			change_variable = { which = fear_actions value = -20 }
			war_lost_lose_authority_effect = yes
		}
		ROOT = {
			participation_scaled_prestige = 100
			hidden_tooltip = {
				disband_event_forces = faction_revolters
			}
		}
		any_attacker = {
			limit = { NOT = { character = ROOT } }
			hidden_tooltip = {
				participation_scaled_prestige = 100
				disband_event_forces = faction_revolters
			}
		}
	}

	on_add_title = {
		e_rebels = {
			persistent_event_target:chronicle_player = {
				if = {
					limit = { character = ROOT }
					chronicle = {
						entry = CHRONICLE_WAR_SENIORITY_ATTACKER
						portrait = [From.GetID]
					}
					break = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { character = FROM }
					chronicle = {
						entry = CHRONICLE_WAR_SENIORITY_DEFENDER
						portrait = [Root.GetID]
					}
					break = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_liege_or_above = ROOT }
					chronicle = {
						entry = CHRONICLE_WAR_SENIORITY_ATTACKER_LIEGE
						portrait = [Root.GetID]
					}
					break = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_liege_or_above = FROM }
					chronicle = {
						entry = CHRONICLE_WAR_SENIORITY_DEFENDER_LIEGE
						portrait = [From.GetID]
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	on_success_title = {
		succession_w_cooldown = seniority
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					NOR = {
						agnatic_culture_trigger = yes
						true_cognatic_culture_trigger = yes
						enatic_culture_trigger = yes
					}
				}
			}
			gender_succ = cognatic
		}
		if = {
			limit = { ROOT = { agnatic_culture_trigger = yes } }
			gender_succ = agnatic
		}
		if = {
			limit = { ROOT = { true_cognatic_culture_trigger = yes } }
			gender_succ = true_cognatic
		}
		if = {
			limit = { ROOT = { enatic_culture_trigger = yes } }
			gender_succ = enatic_cognatic
		}
	}

	on_fail = {
		ROOT = {
			prestige = -100
		}
		FROM = {
			participation_scaled_prestige = 50
		}
		any_defender = {
			limit = { NOT = { character = FROM } }
			hidden_tooltip = { participation_scaled_prestige = 50 }
		}

		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_attacker = {
				disband_event_forces = faction_revolters
				add_character_modifier = {
					name = faction_succ_seniority_ultimatum_timer
					hidden = yes
					duration = 3650
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = { hidden_tooltip = { disband_event_forces = faction_loyalists } }
	}

	on_reverse_demand = {
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				add_character_modifier = { name = victory_timer duration = 3 }
				change_variable = { which = fear_actions value = 10 }
				remove_character_modifier = defeated_major_revolt
				add_character_modifier = { name = defeated_major_revolt duration = 3650 }
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			prestige = -200
			prisoner = FROM
		}
		FROM = {
			participation_scaled_prestige = 100
		}
		any_defender = {
			limit = { NOT = { character = FROM } }
			hidden_tooltip = { participation_scaled_prestige = 100 }
		}

		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_attacker = {
				limit = { liege = { character = FROM } }
				prisoner = FROM
				disband_event_forces = faction_revolters
				add_character_modifier = {
					name = faction_succ_seniority_ultimatum_timer
					hidden = yes
					duration = 3650
				}
			}
			mega_war_emperor_rebels_resolution_effect = yes
		}

		FROM = { hidden_tooltip = { disband_event_forces = faction_loyalists } }
	}

	attacker_ai_victory_worth = {
		factor = -1 # always accept
	}

	attacker_ai_defeat_worth = {
		factor = 100
	}

	defender_ai_victory_worth = {
		factor = -1 # always accept
	}

	defender_ai_defeat_worth = {
		factor = 100
	}
}

invasion = {
	name = CB_NAME_INVASION
	war_name = WAR_NAME_INVASION
	sprite = 7
	truce_days = 3650
	hostile_against_others = yes
	can_ask_to_join_war = no
	allowed_to_target_tributaries = no

	infamy_modifier = 0

	defender_unoccupied_warscore = yes

	sort_priority = 8000

	can_use_title = {
		universal_cb_restrictions_trigger = yes
		universal_cb_title_restrictions_trigger = yes
		OR = {
			FROM = { has_landed_title = PREV }
			holder_scope = { is_liege_or_above = FROM }
		}
	}

	is_valid_title = {
		universal_cb_valid_restrictions_trigger = yes
		OR = {
			FROM = { has_landed_title = PREV }
			holder_scope = { is_liege_or_above = FROM }
		}
	}

	on_add_title = {
		hidden_tooltip = { FROM = { character_event = { id = diplomatic.3099 } } } #call for aid?
		e_rebels = {
			persistent_event_target:chronicle_player = {
				if = {
					limit = { character = ROOT }
					chronicle = {
						entry = CHRONICLE_WAR_INVASION_ATTACKER
						portrait = [From.GetID]
					}
					break = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { character = FROM }
					chronicle = {
						entry = CHRONICLE_WAR_INVASION_DEFENDER
						portrait = [Root.GetID]
					}
					break = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_liege_or_above = ROOT }
					chronicle = {
						entry = CHRONICLE_WAR_INVASION_ATTACKER_LIEGE
						portrait = [Root.GetID]
					}
					break = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_liege_or_above = FROM }
					chronicle = {
						entry = CHRONICLE_WAR_INVASION_DEFENDER_LIEGE
						portrait = [From.GetID]
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	on_success = {
		hidden_tooltip = { ROOT = { add_character_modifier = { name = victory_timer duration = 3 } } }
		ROOT = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_landed_title = k_volantis
					has_global_flag = volantis_rhoynar_invasion
				}
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = TOOLTIPvolantis_rhoynar_invasion
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = {
							capital_scope = { save_event_target_as = rhoynar_capital }
							imprison = ROOT
							clr_character_flag = captured_in_battle
							any_realm_character = {
								limit = {
									at_location = event_target:rhoynar_capital
									NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
								}
								imprison = ROOT
								clr_character_flag = captured_in_battle
							}
						}
						event_target:rhoynar_capital = { #make capital a ruin
							make_province_ruin_effect = yes
						}
						417 = { #Change to Volantis culture/religion
							FROM = {
								any_realm_province = {
									limit = { culture = rhoynar }
									culture = PREVPREV
									religion = PREVPREV
								}
							}
						}
						FROM = {
							any_realm_lord = {
								limit = { NOT = { culture_group = ROOT } }
								any_demesne_title = {
									limit = { controls_religion = no }
									if = {
										limit = { dejure_liege_title = { title = d_orange_shore } }
										d_orange_shore = { de_jure_liege = k_volantis }
									}
									if = {
										limit = { dejure_liege_title = { title = d_valonsar } }
										d_valonsar = { de_jure_liege = k_volantis }
									}
									if = {
										limit = { dejure_liege_title = { title = d_volantene_disputed_lands } }
										d_volantene_disputed_lands = { de_jure_liege = k_volantis }
									}
									usurp_title_plus_barony_if_unlanded = { target = ROOT type = invasion }

								}
							}
							any_demesne_title = {
								limit = { controls_religion = no }
								if = {
									limit = { dejure_liege_title = { title = d_orange_shore } }
									d_orange_shore = { de_jure_liege = k_volantis }
								}
								if = {

									d_volantene_disputed_lands = { de_jure_liege = k_volantis }
								}

							}
						}
						character_event = { id = valyria.151 days = 1 } #potential rhoynar counter invasion
					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					culture = rhoynar
					has_global_flag = volantis_rhoynar_counter_invasion
				}
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = TOOLTIPvolantis_rhoynar_counter_invasion
					hidden_tooltip = {
						FROM = {
							capital_scope = { save_event_target_as = enemy_capital }
							imprison = ROOT
							clr_character_flag = captured_in_battle
							any_realm_character = {
								limit = {
									at_location = event_target:enemy_capital
									NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
								}
								imprison = ROOT
								clr_character_flag = captured_in_battle
							}
							any_realm_province = { #make colonies ruins
								limit = {
									OR = {
										province_id = event_target:enemy_capital
										AND = {
											region = world_the_rhoyne

												culture_group = valyrian

											}
										}
									}
								}
								set_province_flag = ruined_province
								make_province_ruin_effect = yes
							}
						}
						FROM = {
							any_realm_lord = {
								limit = { NOT = { culture_group = ROOT } }
								any_demesne_title = {
									limit = { controls_religion = no }
									if = {
										limit = { dejure_liege_title = { title = d_orange_shore } }
										d_orange_shore = { de_jure_liege = k_rhoynar }
									}
									if = {

									}

										limit = { dejure_liege_title = { title = d_volantene_disputed_lands } }

									}
									usurp_title_plus_barony_if_unlanded = { target = ROOT type = invasion }

								}
							}
							any_demesne_title = {
								limit = { controls_religion = no }
								if = {
									limit = { dejure_liege_title = { title = d_orange_shore } }
									d_orange_shore = { de_jure_liege = k_rhoynar }
								}
								if = {
									limit = { dejure_liege_title = { title = d_valonsar } }
									d_valonsar = { de_jure_liege = k_rhoynar }

					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = andal_adventurer }

								}
							}

		}

					}
				}
			}
		}

		FROM = {

		}
	}

	on_success_title = {

					has_global_flag = volantis_rhoynar_counter_invasion
				}
			}

		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { ROOT = { has_character_flag = andal_adventurer } }

				ROOT = {

					set_defacto_liege = event_target:rebel_andal_backer
					clr_character_flag = andal_adventurer
				}
			}
			else = {
				holder_scope = { #add a marriage to relative of holder
					random_realm_character = {
						limit = {
							is_female = yes
							dynasty = PREV
							OR = {
								character = PREV
								sibling = PREV
								is_child_of = PREV
							}
							age = 10
							NOT = { age = 30 }
							OR = {
								can_marry_trigger = yes
								is_betrothed = yes
								is_married = yes
							}
							is_pregnant = no
							NOT = { trait = celibate }
							NOT = { trait = inbred }
							NOT = { has_character_flag = married_an_andal_invader } #can only do this once
						}
						hidden_tooltip = {
							any_spouse = {
								limit = { is_alive = yes }
								remove_spouse = PREV
							}
						}
						set_character_flag = no_wedding_event
						religion = the_seven
						child_fertility_debuff = yes
						set_character_flag = married_an_andal_invader
						ROOT = {
							hidden_tooltip = {
								any_spouse = {
									limit = { is_alive = yes }
									remove_spouse = PREV
								}
							}
							set_character_flag = no_wedding_event
							if = {
								limit = { has_character_flag = canon_andal_dynasty }
								add_spouse = PREV
							}
							else = {
								add_spouse_matrilineal = PREV
							}
							clr_character_flag = no_wedding_event
						}
						clr_character_flag = no_wedding_event
					}
				}
				if = { #If this is targetting a Empire, shatter it if weak
					limit = {
						FROM = {
							tier = EMPEROR
							primary_title = {
								title = PREVPREV
								OR = {
									has_law = centralization_0
									has_law = centralization_1
								}
							}
							OR = {
								is_adult = no
								is_incapable = yes
								prisoner = yes
								check_variable = { which = tyrant value = 15 }
								primary_title = { has_law = centralization_0 }
							}
						}
					}
					FROM = {
						custom_tooltip = {
							text = TOOLTIPandal_invasion_SHATTER
							hidden_tooltip = {
								#Vassalise split rulers

									limit = {
										NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }

											ROOT_FROM = {

													tier = EMPEROR
													is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV }
												}
											}
											check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0.9 }
										}
									}
									set_defacto_liege = ROOT_FROM
								}
								any_demesne_title = {
									limit = {
										OR = {
											tier = COUNT
											tier = DUKE
										}
									}
									set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 0 }
									set_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0 }
								}
								any_realm_lord = {
									any_demesne_title = {
										limit = {
											OR = {
												tier = COUNT
												tier = DUKE
											}
										}
										set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 0 }
										set_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0 }
									}
								}

								any_demesne_title = {
									limit = { tier = EMPEROR }
									destroy_landed_title = THIS
								}
								any_realm_lord = {
									character_event = { id = andal.7 days = 1 }
								}
								any_courtier = {
									limit = {
										is_ruler = no
										culture_group = ROOT
										religion = ROOT
										NOT = { trait = zealous }
									}
									religion = the_seven
								}

							set_defacto_liege = ROOT
							character_event = { id = maintenance.25 } #Subjugation flag maintenance
						}
					}
				}
				else_if = { #if primary title of target, take whole realm

						tooltip = { set_defacto_liege = ROOT }
						if = {

							set_defacto_liege = ROOT
							character_event = { id = maintenance.25 } #Subjugation flag maintenance
						}
					}
				}
				else = {

								}

							set_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0 }
						}

								limit = {
									OR = {
										tier = COUNT
										tier = DUKE
									}
								}
								set_variable = { which = "de_facto_kingdom" value = 0 }
								set_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0 }
							}
						}

							succession = primogeniture
							gender_succ = cognatic
						}

							limit = {
								can_marry_trigger = yes

								limit = {
									is_ruler = no

											NOT = { tier = BARON }

										is_betrothed = yes
									}

									NOT = { age = 30 }
									is_pregnant = no
									NOT = { trait = celibate }
									NOT = { trait = inbred }
									NOT = { has_character_flag = married_an_andal_invader } #can only do this once

			limit = {

						character_event = { id = maintenance.21 } #Take dejure vassals (AGOT)

					}

					has_global_flag = andal_invasion_of_norvos

				}

			}
		}
		if = { #Ghiscari Wars
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					has_landed_title = e_ghiscar
					has_global_flag = ghiscari_war
				}
				FROM = {
					has_landed_title = e_new_valyria
				}
			}
			clr_global_flag = ghiscari_war
		}
	}

	on_fail = {
		ROOT = {
			prestige = -200
			hidden_tooltip = { disband_event_forces = summer_islanders }
			clr_character_flag = unite_shadowlander_war
			hidden_tooltip = {
				any_realm_province = {
					limit = { has_province_flag = former_shadowlander_province }
					clr_province_flag = former_shadowlander_province
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_global_flag = andal_invasion_of_norvos
					has_landed_title = e_andalos
				}
				clr_global_flag = andal_invasion_of_norvos
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			prestige = 100
		}
		FROM = {
			participation_scaled_prestige = 100
		}
		any_defender = {
			limit = { NOT = { character = FROM } }
			hidden_tooltip = { participation_scaled_prestige = 100 }
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					has_landed_title = k_volantis
					has_global_flag = volantis_rhoynar_invasion
				}
			}
			clr_global_flag = volantis_rhoynar_invasion
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					culture = rhoynar
					has_global_flag = volantis_rhoynar_counter_invasion
				}
			}
			clr_global_flag = volantis_rhoynar_counter_invasion
		}
		if = {
			limit = { ROOT = { has_character_flag = andal_adventurer } }
			any_attacker = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = rebel_andal_backer }
				clr_character_flag = rebel_andal_backer
			}
			ROOT = {
				hidden_tooltip = {
					any_demesne_title = {
						limit = { is_landless_type_title = yes }
						activate_title = { status = no title = THIS }
						destroy_landed_title = THIS
					}
				}
				clr_character_flag = andal_adventurer
			}
		}
		if = { #Ghiscari Wars
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					has_landed_title = e_ghiscar
					has_global_flag = ghiscari_war
				}
				FROM = {
					has_landed_title = e_new_valyria
				}
			}
			clr_global_flag = ghiscari_war
		}
	}

	on_reverse_demand = {
		hidden_tooltip = { FROM = { add_character_modifier = { name = victory_timer duration = 3 } } }
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					culture = rhoynar
					has_global_flag = volantis_rhoynar_counter_invasion
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = TOOLTIPvolantis_rhoynar_counter_invasionB
				hidden_tooltip = {
					k_rhoynar = { de_jure_liege = e_new_valyria }
					#Find ten thousand ships leader
					any_attacker = {
						limit = {
							NOT = { character = ROOT }
							culture = rhoynar
							is_adult = yes
							prisoner = no
							is_incapable = no
							OR = {
								martial = 12
								diplomacy = 12
								prestige = 1000
							}
						}
						save_event_target_as = ten_thousand_ships_leader
					}
					any_attacker = { #player
						limit = {
							NOT = { character = ROOT }
							culture = rhoynar
							is_adult = yes
							prisoner = no
							is_incapable = no
							ai = no
						}
						save_event_target_as = ten_thousand_ships_leader
					}
					c_2000001 = { #Nymeria
						if = {
							limit = {
								is_alive = yes
								independent = yes
								is_adult = yes
								prisoner = no
								is_incapable = no
								NOT = { character = ROOT }
							}
							save_event_target_as = ten_thousand_ships_leader
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { event_target:ten_thousand_ships_leader = { always = yes } } }
						random_character = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { character = ROOT }
								culture = rhoynar
								is_adult = yes
								prisoner = no
								is_incapable = no
								martial = 12
								diplomacy = 12
								OR = {
									is_lowborn = no
									prestige = 300
								}
								can_press_claims_trigger = yes
							}
							save_event_target_as = ten_thousand_ships_leader
						}
					}
					if = {
						limit = { NOT = { event_target:ten_thousand_ships_leader = { always = yes } } }
						random_list = {
							50 = {
								create_random_soldier = {
									random_traits = yes
									culture = rhoynar
									religion = rhoynar_pagan
									dynasty = actually_culture
									female = no
									historical = yes
								}
							}
							50 = {
								create_random_soldier = {
									random_traits = yes
									culture = rhoynar
									religion = rhoynar_pagan
									dynasty = actually_culture
									female = yes
									historical = yes
								}
							}
						}
						new_character = {
							save_event_target_as = ten_thousand_ships_leader
							random_list = {
								20 = { add_trait = master_warrior }
								40 = { add_trait = skilled_warrior }
								40 = { add_trait = trained_warrior }
							}
							remove_trait = weak
							remove_trait = slow
							remove_trait = imbecile
							remove_trait = dull
							random_list = { # Flavor Randomization
								35 = {
									# Nothing
								}
								15 = {
									change_martial = 2
								}
								10 = {
									trigger = { NOT = { trait = strong } }
									add_trait = robust
								}
								10 = {
									add_trait = duelist
								}
								10 = {
									add_trait = hunter
								}
								5 = {
									add_trait = strategist
								}
								5 = {
									change_martial = 4
								}
								5 = {
									if = {
										limit = {
											has_dlc = "Reapers"
										}
										add_trait = one_eyed
									}
								}
								5 = {
									trigger = {
										is_smart_incl_genius_trigger = no
									}
									add_trait = shrewd
								}
							}
							while = {
								limit = { martial < 10 }
								change_martial = 1
							}
							while = {
								limit = { diplomacy < 10 }
								change_diplomacy = 1
							}
							wealth = 100
						}
					}
					event_target:ten_thousand_ships_leader = {
						create_title = {
							tier = DUKE
							landless = yes
							#temporary = yes
							#adventurer = yes
							culture = event_target:ten_thousand_ships_leader
							name = "TEN_THOUSAND_SHIPS_HOST"

						save_event_target_as = volantis
					}
					any_attacker = {
						limit = { culture = rhoynar }
						capital_scope = { save_event_target_as = rhoynar_capital }
						if = {
							limit = { NOT = { character = event_target:ten_thousand_ships_leader } }
							imprison = FROM
							set_character_flag = captured_in_battle
						}
						any_realm_character = {
							limit = {
								at_location = event_target:rhoynar_capital
								NOT = { character = event_target:ten_thousand_ships_leader }
								NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
							}
							imprison = FROM
							set_character_flag = captured_in_battle
						}
						any_realm_character = {
							limit = {
								NOT = { at_location = event_target:rhoynar_capital }
								NOT = { character = event_target:ten_thousand_ships_leader }
								NOT = { is_inaccessible_trigger = yes }
							}
							random = {
								chance = 33
								imprison = FROM
								set_character_flag = captured_in_battle
							}
						}
						any_realm_lord = {
							any_demesne_title = {
								limit = {
									controls_religion = no
									is_landless_type_title = no
									lower_tier_than = DUKE
									location = {
										NOR = {
											kingdom = { title = k_rhoynar }
											duchy = { title = d_orange_shore }
											duchy = { title = d_valonsar }
											duchy = { title = d_volantene_disputed_lands }
											province_id = 450 #Ghoyan Drohe
											province_id = 421 #Sar Mell
										}
									}
								}
								usurp_title_plus_barony_if_unlanded = { target = FROM type = invasion }
							}
						}
						any_demesne_title = {
							limit = {
								controls_religion = no
								is_landless_type_title = no
								lower_tier_than = DUKE
								location = {
									NOR = {
										kingdom = { title = k_rhoynar }
										duchy = { title = d_orange_shore }
										duchy = { title = d_valonsar }
										duchy = { title = d_volantene_disputed_lands }
										province_id = 450 #Ghoyan Drohe
										province_id = 421 #Sar Mell
									}
								}
							}
							usurp_title_plus_barony_if_unlanded = { target = FROM type = invasion }
						}

							limit = {
								culture = rhoynar
								NOT = { duchy = { title = d_orange_shore } }
								NOT = { duchy = { title = d_valonsar } }
								NOT = { duchy = { title = d_volantene_disputed_lands } }
							}
							if = {
								limit = { province_id = 450 }
								d_velvet_hills = { de_jure_liege = k_pentos }
							}
							set_province_flag = ruined_province
							make_province_ruin_effect = yes
						}
						any_realm_province = {
							limit = { culture = rhoynar }
							culture = event_target:volantis
							religion = event_target:volantis
						}
						any_realm_lord = {
							limit = { NOT = { culture_group = FROM } }
							any_demesne_title = {
								limit = {
									controls_religion = no
									is_landless_type_title = no
									higher_tier_than = COUNT
								}
								destroy_landed_title = THIS
							}
							any_demesne_title = {
								limit = {
									controls_religion = no
									is_landless_type_title = no
								}
								if = {
									limit = { dejure_liege_title = { title = d_orange_shore } }
									d_orange_shore = { de_jure_liege = k_volantis }
								}
								if = {
									limit = { dejure_liege_title = { title = d_valonsar } }
									d_valonsar = { de_jure_liege = k_volantis }
								}
								if = {
									limit = { dejure_liege_title = { title = d_volantene_disputed_lands } }
									d_volantene_disputed_lands = { de_jure_liege = k_volantis }
								}
								usurp_title_plus_barony_if_unlanded = { target = FROM type = invasion }

							}
						}
						any_demesne_title = {
							limit = {
								controls_religion = no
								is_landless_type_title = no
								higher_tier_than = COUNT
							}
							destroy_landed_title = THIS
						}
						any_demesne_title = {
							limit = {
								controls_religion = no
								is_landless_type_title = no
							}
							if = {
								limit = { dejure_liege_title = { title = d_orange_shore } }

							}
							if = {
								limit = { dejure_liege_title = { title = d_valonsar } }
								d_valonsar = { de_jure_liege = k_volantis }
							}
							if = {
								limit = { dejure_liege_title = { title = d_volantene_disputed_lands } }
								d_volantene_disputed_lands = { de_jure_liege = k_volantis }
							}
							usurp_title_plus_barony_if_unlanded = { target = FROM type = invasion }

		if = {
			limit = { ROOT = { has_character_flag = andal_adventurer } }
			any_attacker = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = rebel_andal_backer }

						limit = { is_landless_type_title = yes }

						destroy_landed_title = THIS
					}
				}
				clr_character_flag = andal_adventurer
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				FROM = {
					add_character_modifier = { #Usually a 10 year cooldown on next invasion
						name = defeated_an_andal_invasion
						duration = 3650
					}

		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					has_global_flag = andal_invasion_of_norvos
					has_landed_title = e_andalos
				}

			e_andalos = { destroy_landed_title = THIS }
			ROOT = { imprison = FROM }
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = TOOLTIPandal_invasion_of_norvos

							limit = {
								tier = KING

									check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 1 }

								limit = { higher_tier_than = DUKE }

							}

							limit = { tier = KING }
							any_demesne_title = {
								limit = { higher_tier_than = DUKE }

							limit = { higher_tier_than = COUNT }
							destroy_landed_title = THIS

							}
							make_province_ruin_effect = yes
						}
					}
					clr_global_flag = andal_invasion_of_norvos

		else_if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					primary_title = {
						has_title_flag = andal_counter_invasion_title
						ROOT = { has_claim = PREV }

				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				any_demesne_title = {
					limit = { tier = EMPEROR }

						if = { #establish the mountain clans
							limit = {

			hidden_tooltip = {
				FROM = {
					any_demesne_title = {
						limit = { has_title_flag = andal_counter_invasion_title }
						any_independent_ruler = { #change mega war variable
							limit = {
								primary_title = { check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 1 } }

									has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT_FROM modifier = opinion_de_facto_liege }

										check_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV }

								NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT_FROM modifier = opinion_granted_independence } }

								limit = {
									NOT = { tier = BARON }
									NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
								}
								set_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = event_target:new_primary_title }

							character_event = { id = diplomatic.51 days = 10 } #check royal privilege
						}
						destroy_landed_title = THIS

					any_vassal = {
						limit = { tier = KING }
						character_event = { id = diplomatic.51 days = 2 } #check royal privilege
					}
					character_event = { id = andal.2 days = 50 } #check andal invasion status
				}
			}
		}
		if = { #Ghiscari Wars
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					has_landed_title = e_ghiscar
					has_global_flag = ghiscari_war
				}

					has_landed_title = e_new_valyria
				}

				limit = {
					ROOT = {

							county = {

			ROOT = {

					}
				}

		}

			prestige = -200

			if = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = summer_islander_invader }

				clr_character_flag = summer_islander_invader
			}

							}

						}
					}
				}

			prestige = 200
		}
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = maintenance.2199 tooltip = TOOLTIPmaintenance.2199 } #Take back dejure vassals (AGOT)

		}

			mega_war_emperor_rebels_resolution_effect = yes

		}
	}

	on_reverse_demand_title = {
		ROOT = { show_scope_change = no remove_claim = PREV }
	}

		if = {
			limit = {

					}

							limit = { is_landless_type_title = yes }

							destroy_landed_title = THIS

			end_war = whitepeace
		}
	}

	on_invalidation = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					has_landed_title = k_volantis
					has_global_flag = volantis_rhoynar_invasion
				}
			}
			clr_global_flag = volantis_rhoynar_invasion
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					culture = rhoynar
					has_global_flag = volantis_rhoynar_counter_invasion
				}
			}
			clr_global_flag = volantis_rhoynar_counter_invasion
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { ROOT = { has_character_flag = andal_adventurer } }
			any_attacker = {
				limit = { has_character_flag = rebel_andal_backer }
				clr_character_flag = rebel_andal_backer
			}
			ROOT = {
				hidden_tooltip = {
					any_demesne_title = {
						limit = { is_landless_type_title = yes }
						activate_title = { status = no title = THIS }
						destroy_landed_title = THIS
					}
				}
				clr_character_flag = andal_adventurer
			}
		}
		else_if = { #Ghiscari Wars
			limit = {
				ROOT = {
					has_landed_title = e_ghiscar
					has_global_flag = ghiscari_war
				}
				FROM = {
					has_landed_title = e_new_valyria
				}
			}
			clr_global_flag = ghiscari_war
		}
	}

tribal_invasion = {
	name = CB_NAME_INVASION
	war_name = WAR_NAME_INVASION
	sprite = 8
	truce_days = 3650
	hostile_against_others = yes
	is_permanent = yes
	can_ask_to_join_war = yes
	check_de_jure_tier = KING # this scans all de jure kingdoms for the counties which are held by or vassals(or below) of selected character. Only valid if is_permanent = yes
	allowed_to_target_tributaries = no

	infamy_modifier = 0

	sort_priority = 8000

	can_use_gui = {
		ROOT = {
			prestige = 500
		}
		# custom_tooltip = {
			# text = TOOLTIPCBENFORCEDTRUCE
			# hidden_tooltip = {
				# FROM = {
					# NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_enforced_truce } }
				# }
			# }
		# }
	}

	can_use_title = {
		universal_cb_restrictions_trigger = yes
		universal_cb_title_restrictions_trigger = yes
		ROOT = {
			OR = {
				ai = yes
				multiplayer = no
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = {
						name = multiplayer_invasions
						value = off
					}
				}
			}
			OR = {
				AND = {
					independent = yes
					#OR = {
						#religion_group = pagan_group
						#AND = {
							OR = {
								has_horde_culture = yes
								has_character_flag = horde_invader
								culture = moon_clansman
								culture = gendels_folk
							}
							#NOT = { religion_group = christian }
						#}
					#}
					#OR = {
						#culture_group = altaic
						#culture_group = magyar
					#}
					higher_tier_than = COUNT
					#OR = {
						#has_horde_culture = yes
						#has_character_flag = horde_invader
						#FROM = {
							#NOT = { religion_group = pagan_group } # Should subjugate these instead
						#}
					#}
				}

				AND = {
					mercenary = yes
					NOT = {
						num_of_titles = 2
					}
				}
				AND = {
					has_character_flag = is_child_of_destiny
					any_owned_bloodline = {
						has_bloodline_flag = founder_invasions
					}
				}
				AND = {
					NOT = { has_character_flag = flag_declared_bloodline_invasion }
					any_owned_bloodline = {
						has_bloodline_flag = bloodline_great_conquerors
					}
				}
			}
		}

		ROOT = {
			NOT = { same_realm = FROM }
		}
	}

	is_valid_title = {
		FROM = {
			any_realm_province = {
				de_jure_liege_or_above = PREVPREV
			}
		}
	}

	on_add = {
		ROOT = { prestige = -500 }
		hidden_tooltip = { FROM = { character_event = { id = diplomatic.3099 } } } #call for aid?
		if = {
			limit = {
				attacker = {
					any_owned_bloodline = {
						has_bloodline_flag = bloodline_great_conquerors
					}
				}
			}
			attacker = {
				set_character_flag = flag_declared_bloodline_invasion
			}
		}
	}

	on_add_title = {
		e_rebels = {
			persistent_event_target:chronicle_player = {
				if = {
					limit = { character = ROOT }
					chronicle = {
						entry = CHRONICLE_WAR_INVASION_ATTACKER
						portrait = [From.GetID]
					}
					break = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { character = FROM }
					chronicle = {
						entry = CHRONICLE_WAR_INVASION_DEFENDER
						portrait = [Root.GetID]
					}
					break = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_liege_or_above = ROOT }
					chronicle = {
						entry = CHRONICLE_WAR_INVASION_ATTACKER_LIEGE
						portrait = [Root.GetID]
					}
					break = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_liege_or_above = FROM }
					chronicle = {
						entry = CHRONICLE_WAR_INVASION_DEFENDER_LIEGE
						portrait = [From.GetID]
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	on_success = {
		hidden_tooltip = { ROOT = { add_character_modifier = { name = victory_timer duration = 3 } } }
		ROOT = {
			prestige = 200
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_landed_title = k_mountain_clans
					has_character_flag = moon_clansman_invader
				}
				clr_character_flag = moon_clansman_invader
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			participation_scaled_prestige = 200
		}
		any_attacker = {
			limit = { NOT = { character = ROOT } }
			hidden_tooltip = { participation_scaled_prestige = 200 }
		}
		FROM = {
			prestige = -200
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			ROOT = {
				occupy_minors_of_occupied_settlements = FROM
				gain_all_occupied_titles = { who = FROM type = invasion }

				if = {
					limit = {
						has_nickname = no
					}
					random_list = {
						150 = { }
						10 = { give_nickname = nick_the_great }
						10 = { give_nickname = nick_the_victorious }
						10 = { give_nickname = nick_the_conqueror }
						10 = { give_nickname = nick_the_brave }
						10 = { give_nickname = nick_the_dragon }
						10 = { give_nickname = nick_the_terrible }
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	on_success_title = {
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = tribal_invasion_succ_tip
			hidden_tooltip = {
				ROOT = {
					vassalize_or_take_under_title_destroy_duchies = {
						title = PREV
						enemy = FROM
						is_crusade = yes # Even if the title holder is not participating in the war, gain holdings occupied by all Crusade participants
						type = invasion
					}
				}
				FROM = {
					if = {
						limit = { lower_tier_than = ROOT is_ruler = yes }
						set_defacto_liege = ROOT
						character_event = { id = maintenance.25 } #Subjugation flag maintenance
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						e_mexikha = {
							holder = ROOT
						}
					}
					ROOT = {
						any_realm_province = {
							limit = {
								OR = {
									has_province_flag = aztec_explorers
									has_province_flag = aztec_second_wave
								}
							}
							religion = aztec
							clr_province_flag = aztec_explorers
							clr_province_flag = aztec_second_wave
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	on_fail = {
		FROM = {
			prestige = 100
		}
		FROM = {
			participation_scaled_prestige = 100
		}
		any_defender = {
			limit = { NOT = { character = FROM } }
			hidden_tooltip = { participation_scaled_prestige = 100 }
		}
		ROOT = {
			prestige = -200
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_landed_title = k_mountain_clans
					has_character_flag = moon_clansman_invader
				}
				clr_character_flag = moon_clansman_invader
				hidden_tooltip = { activate_title = { status = no title = k_mountain_clans } }
				k_mountain_clans = { destroy_landed_title = THIS }
				hidden_tooltip = { disband_event_forces = clansmen_troops }
			}
		}
	}

	on_reverse_demand = {
		hidden_tooltip = { FROM = { add_character_modifier = { name = victory_timer duration = 3 } } }
		ROOT = {
			prestige = -200
			transfer_scaled_wealth = {
				to = FROM
				value = 4.0
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_landed_title = k_mountain_clans
					has_character_flag = moon_clansman_invader
				}
				clr_character_flag = moon_clansman_invader
				hidden_tooltip = { activate_title = { status = no title = k_mountain_clans } }
				k_mountain_clans = { destroy_landed_title = THIS }
				hidden_tooltip = { disband_event_forces = clansmen_troops }
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			prestige = 200

			hidden_tooltip = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_nickname = no
					}
					random_list = {
						200 = { }
						10 = { give_nickname = nick_the_great }
						10 = { give_nickname = nick_the_hammer }
						10 = { give_nickname = nick_the_avenger }
						10 = { give_nickname = nick_the_lion }
						10 = { give_nickname = nick_the_bold }
					}
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			character_event = { id = maintenance.2199 tooltip = TOOLTIPmaintenance.2199 } #Take back dejure vassals (AGOT)
			participation_scaled_prestige = 200
		}
		any_defender = {
			limit = { NOT = { character = FROM } }
			hidden_tooltip = { participation_scaled_prestige = 200 }
		}
	}

	on_attacker_leader_death = {
		ROOT = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_landed_title = k_mountain_clans
					has_character_flag = moon_clansman_invader
				}
				current_heir = { set_character_flag = moon_clansman_invader }
			}
		}
	}

	attacker_ai_victory_worth = {
		factor = 200
	}

	attacker_ai_defeat_worth = {
		factor = 100
	}

	defender_ai_victory_worth = {
		factor = -1 # always accept
	}

	defender_ai_defeat_worth = {
		factor = 100
	}

	# ai importance placed on this CB: scope is the targeted title, ROOT is the attacking character, FROM is the defending character
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 2

		#Dragon intimidation
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			ROOT = {
				NOT = { can_use_dragon_abilities_trigger = yes }
				NOT = { relative_power = { who = FROM power = 6 } }
			}
			FROM = {
				can_use_dragon_abilities_trigger = yes
				OR = {
					any_friend = { trait = dragon martial = 60 }
					AND = {  graphical_culture = dragongfx martial = 60 }
				}
				is_incapable = no
			}
		}
	}
}

excommunicated_ruler = {
	name = CB_NAME_EXCOMMUNICATED_RULER
	war_name = WAR_NAME_EXCOMMUNICATED_RULER
	sprite = 11
	truce_days = 3650

	is_permanent = yes
	can_ask_to_join_war = no
	allowed_to_target_tributaries = no

	defender_unoccupied_warscore = yes

	infamy_modifier = 0

	sort_priority = 4500

	can_use_gui = {
		# custom_tooltip = {
			# text = TOOLTIPCBENFORCEDTRUCE
			# hidden_tooltip = {
				# FROM = {
					# NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_enforced_truce } }
				# }
			# }
		# }
	}

	can_use = {
		universal_cb_restrictions_trigger = yes
		ROOT = {
			religion = the_seven
			crownlaw_title = { has_law = investiture_law_3 }
			NOT = { excommunicated_for = ROOT }
		}
		FROM = {
			excommunicated_for = ROOT
			religion = the_seven
			in_revolt = no
			NOT = {
				any_current_enemy = {
					NOT = {
						religion_group = ROOT
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	is_valid = {
		universal_cb_valid_restrictions_trigger = yes
		FROM = {
			excommunicated_for = ROOT
		}
		OR = {
			ROOT = { has_character_flag = flag_excommunicated_for_coronation }
			ROOT = { NOT = { excommunicated_for = ROOT } }
		}
	}

	on_add = {
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							is_theocracy = yes
							is_republic = yes
						}
					}
					character_event = { id = diplomatic.3099 } #call for aid?
				}
			}
		}
		e_rebels = {
			persistent_event_target:chronicle_player = {
				if = {
					limit = { character = ROOT }
					chronicle = {
						entry = CHRONICLE_WAR_EXCOMMUNICATION_ATTACKER
						portrait = [From.GetID]
					}
					break = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { character = FROM }
					chronicle = {
						entry = CHRONICLE_WAR_EXCOMMUNICATION_DEFENDER
						portrait = [Root.GetID]
					}
					break = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_liege_or_above = ROOT }
					chronicle = {
						entry = CHRONICLE_WAR_EXCOMMUNICATION_ATTACKER_LIEGE
						portrait = [Root.GetID]
					}
					break = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_liege_or_above = FROM }
					chronicle = {
						entry = CHRONICLE_WAR_EXCOMMUNICATION_DEFENDER_LIEGE
						portrait = [From.GetID]
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	on_success = {
		hidden_tooltip = {
			ROOT = { add_character_modifier = { name = victory_timer duration = 3 } }
			mega_war_rebel_leader_resolution_effect = yes
			FROM = { change_variable = { which = fear_actions value = -20 } }
			if = {
				limit = {
					ROOT = { has_character_flag = flag_excommunicated_for_coronation }
				}
				ROOT = {
					character_event = { id = HF.20220 } #Papal Coronation may proceed.
				}
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						primary_title = {
							tier = BARON
						}
					}
				}
				ROOT = {
					piety = 10
					prestige = 50
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						primary_title = {
							tier = COUNT
						}
					}
				}
				ROOT = {
					piety = 20
					prestige = 100
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						primary_title = {
							tier = DUKE
						}
					}
				}
				ROOT = {
					piety = 30
					prestige = 150
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						primary_title = {
							tier = KING
						}
					}
				}
				ROOT = {
					piety = 50
					prestige = 200
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					FROM = {
						primary_title = {
							tier = EMPEROR
						}
					}
				}
				ROOT = {
					piety = 70
					prestige = 400
				}
			}
		}

		FROM = {
			excommunicate = no
			prestige = -200
			war_lost_lose_authority_effect = yes
			rightful_religious_head_scope = {
				opinion = {
					who = PREV
					modifier = opinion_repented_sins
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = { #Universal on death/abdication event
				if = {
					limit = { any_artifact = { has_artifact_flag = valyrian_steel } }
					set_character_flag = do_not_inherit_sword
				}
				set_character_flag = abdication
				character_event = { id = 45341 }
				clr_character_flag = abdication
				clr_character_flag = do_not_inherit_sword
				if = {
					limit = { is_merchant_republic = no }
					current_heir = { save_event_target_as = wealth_heir }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_merchant_republic = yes }
					family_palace = { current_heir = { save_event_target_as = wealth_heir } }
				}
				transfer_scaled_wealth = { to = event_target:wealth_heir value = all }
			}
			abdicate = yes
		}
	}

	on_fail = {
		ROOT = {
			piety = -50
			prestige = -100
		}
	}

	on_reverse_demand = {
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				add_character_modifier = { name = victory_timer duration = 3 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = {
							OR = {
								vassal_of = ROOT_FROM
								liege_before_war = { character = ROOT_FROM }
							}
							OR = {
								higher_tier_than = DUKE
								relative_power_including_allies_attacker = { who = PREV power = 0.3 }
							}
						}
					}
					change_variable = { which = fear_actions value = 10 }
					remove_character_modifier = defeated_major_revolt
					add_character_modifier = { name = defeated_major_revolt duration = 3650 }
				}
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			piety = -100
			prestige = -200
			transfer_scaled_wealth = {
				to = FROM
				value = 4.0
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			prestige = 200
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			mega_war_emperor_rebels_resolution_effect = yes
		}
	}

	# ai importance placed on this CB: scope is the targeted title, ROOT is the attacking character, FROM is the defending character
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1

		#Dragon intimidation
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			ROOT = {
				NOT = { can_use_dragon_abilities_trigger = yes }
				NOT = { relative_power = { who = FROM power = 6 } }
			}
			FROM = {
				can_use_dragon_abilities_trigger = yes
				OR = {
					any_friend = { trait = dragon martial = 60 }
					AND = {  graphical_culture = dragongfx martial = 60 }
				}
				is_incapable = no
			}
		}
	}

	attacker_ai_victory_worth = {
		factor = -1 # always accept
	}

	attacker_ai_defeat_worth = {
		factor = 100
	}

	defender_ai_victory_worth = {
		factor = -1 # always accept
	}

	defender_ai_defeat_worth = {
		factor = 100
	}
}

bid_for_independence = {
	name = CB_NAME_INDEPENDENCE
	war_name = WAR_NAME_INDEPENDENCE
	sprite = 12
	truce_days = 3650

	is_permanent = yes
	is_independence = yes
	attacker_unoccupied_warscore = yes

	infamy_modifier = 0

	sort_priority = 4000

	can_use_gui = {
		# custom_tooltip = {
			# text = TOOLTIPCBENFORCEDTRUCE
			# hidden_tooltip = {
				# FROM = {
					# NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_enforced_truce } }
				# }
			# }
		# }
		custom_tooltip = {
			text = TOOLTIPbid_for_independenceDEJURESUBVASSAL
			hidden_tooltip = {
				NAND = {
					FROM = { de_jure_vassal_or_below = ROOT }
					FROM = { independent = no }
				}
			}
		}
		conditional_tooltip = { #jogos nhai do not make war on eachother
			trigger = { ROOT = { has_jogos_nhai_war_block_trigger = yes } }
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = TOOLTIPJOGOSWARPROHIBITION
				hidden_tooltip = { NOT = { FROM = { has_jogos_nhai_war_block_trigger = yes } } }
			}
		}
	}

	can_use = {
		universal_cb_restrictions_trigger = yes
		ROOT = {
			OR = {
				NOT = { is_nomadic = yes }
				NOT = {
					clan_opinion = { who = FROM value = 0 }
				}
				has_character_flag = refused_nomad_absorption
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			de_facto_liege = FROM

			higher_tier_than = BARON
			OR = {
				ai = yes
				is_feudal = yes
				is_tribal = yes
				higher_tier_than = COUNT
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			FROM = {
				liege = {
					NOT = { character = PREV }
					OR = {
						is_primary_war_attacker = yes
						is_primary_war_defender = yes
					}
				}
			}
		}

		FROM = {
			NOT = {
				any_war = {
					attacker = {
						character = PREVPREV
					}
					OR = {
						using_cb = bid_for_independence
						using_cb = depose_liege
					}
				}
			}
			any_demesne_title = {
				NOT = { lower_tier_than = ROOT }
				temporary = no
			}
		}
	}

	is_valid = {
		ROOT = {
			OR = {
				liege = {
					character = PREV # either independent
				}
				liege = {
					FROM = {
						is_liege_or_above = PREV # or have shared liege
					}
				}
				has_character_flag = post_civil_war_indep_war
			}
			NOT = { has_character_flag = end_indep_wars }
		}
		OR = {
			FROM = {
				any_demesne_title = {
					NOT = { lower_tier_than = ROOT }
					temporary = no
				}
			}
			AND = {
				FROM = { tier = EMPEROR }
				ROOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
			}
		}
	}

	on_add = {
		ROOT = {
			add_character_modifier = {
				name = "indep_war"
				duration = 100
			}
		}
		e_rebels = {
			persistent_event_target:chronicle_player = {
				if = {
					limit = { character = ROOT }
					chronicle = {
						entry = CHRONICLE_WAR_INDEPENDENCE_ATTACKER
						portrait = [From.GetID]
					}
					break = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { character = FROM }
					chronicle = {
						entry = CHRONICLE_WAR_INDEPENDENCE_DEFENDER
						portrait = [Root.GetID]
					}
					break = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_liege_or_above = ROOT }
					chronicle = {
						entry = CHRONICLE_WAR_INDEPENDENCE_ATTACKER_LIEGE
						portrait = [Root.GetID]
					}
					break = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_liege_or_above = FROM }
					chronicle = {
						entry = CHRONICLE_WAR_INDEPENDENCE_DEFENDER_LIEGE
						portrait = [From.GetID]
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	on_success = {
		hidden_tooltip = {
			ROOT = { add_character_modifier = { name = victory_timer duration = 3 } }
			# mega_war_rebel_leader_resolution_effect = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					independent = no
				}
			}
			FROM = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						in_revolt = yes
					}
					liege_before_war = {
						ROOT = {
							set_defacto_liege = PREV
						}
						if = {
							limit = { NOT = { tier = EMPEROR } }
							hidden_tooltip = {
								ROOT = {
									any_demesne_title = {
										limit = {
											NOT = { tier = BARON }
											NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
										}
										set_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0 }
									}
									any_realm_lord = {
										any_demesne_title = {
											limit = {
												NOT = { tier = BARON }
												NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
											}
											set_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0 }
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						in_revolt = no
					}
					liege = {
						ROOT = {
							set_defacto_liege = PREV
						}
						if = {
							limit = { NOT = { tier = EMPEROR } }
							hidden_tooltip = {
								ROOT = {
									any_demesne_title = {
										limit = {
											NOT = { tier = BARON }
											NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
										}
										set_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0 }
									}
									any_realm_lord = {
										any_demesne_title = {
											limit = {
												NOT = { tier = BARON }
												NOT = { tier = EMPEROR }
											}
											set_variable = { which = "de_facto_empire" value = 0 }
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				FROM = {
					independent = yes
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				set_defacto_liege = ROOT
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_character_flag = post_civil_war_indep_war
						lower_tier_than = KING
					}
					character_event = { id = mega_wars.51 tooltip = EVTTOOLTIPmega_wars.51 }
				}
			}
		}

		ROOT = {
			#prestige = 100
			any_demesne_title = {
				limit = {
					tier = ROOT
					controls_religion = no
					NOT = {
						dejure_liege_title = {
							OR = {
								FROM = { has_landed_title = PREV }
								dejure_liege_title = {
									OR = {
										FROM = { has_landed_title = PREV }
										dejure_liege_title = { FROM = { has_landed_title = PREV } }
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
				add_weak_pressed_claim = FROM
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				character_event = { id = mega_wars.50 } #Character wins indep war maintenance
				add_character_modifier = {
					name = "indep_faction_won"
					duration = 20
				}
			}
		}

		ROOT = {
			participation_scaled_prestige = 100
		}
		any_attacker = {
			limit = { NOT = { character = ROOT } }
			hidden_tooltip = {
				participation_scaled_prestige = 100
				if = {
					limit = {
						FROM = { tier = EMPEROR }
						OR = {
							liege_before_war = { character = FROM }
							is_liege_or_above = FROM
							primary_title = {
								FROM = {
									primary_title = {
										is_variable_equal = { which = "de_facto_empire" which = PREVPREV }
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}
					character_event = { id = mega_wars.53 days = 1 }
				}
			}
		}

		FROM = {
			change_variable = { which = fear_actions value = -20 }
			war_lost_lose_authority_effect = yes
		}
	}

	attacker_ai_victory_worth = {
		factor = -1 # always accept
	}

	attacker_ai_defeat_worth = {
		factor = 150
	}

	defender_ai_victory_worth = {
		factor = -1 # always accept
	}

	defender_ai_defeat_worth = {
		factor = 100
	}

	# ai importance placed on this CB: scope is the targeted title, ROOT is the attacking character, FROM is the defending character
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
		#Dragon intimidation
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			ROOT = {
				NOT = { can_use_dragon_abilities_trigger = yes }
				NOT = { relative_power = { who = FROM power = 6 } }
			}
			FROM = {
				can_use_dragon_abilities_trigger = yes
				OR = {
					any_friend = { trait = dragon martial = 60 }
					AND = {  graphical_culture = dragongfx martial = 60 }
				}
				is_incapable = no
			}
		}
	}
}

depose_liege = {
	name = CB_NAME_DEPOSE_LIEGE
	war_name = WAR_NAME_DEPOSE_LIEGE
	sprite = 12
	truce_days = 3650

	is_permanent = yes
	can_call_vassals = no
	major_revolt = no

	infamy_modifier = 0

	sort_priority = 4000

	can_use_gui = {
		# custom_tooltip = {
			# text = TOOLTIPCBENFORCEDTRUCE
			# hidden_tooltip = {
				# FROM = {
					# NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_enforced_truce } }
				# }
			# }
		# }
		conditional_tooltip = { #jogos nhai do not make war on eachother
			trigger = { ROOT = { has_jogos_nhai_war_block_trigger = yes } }
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = TOOLTIPJOGOSWARPROHIBITION
				hidden_tooltip = { NOT = { FROM = { has_jogos_nhai_war_block_trigger = yes } } }
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			is_feudal = yes
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = TOOLTIPdepose_liegeWAR
				hidden_tooltip = {
					NOT = {
						any_war = {
							OR = {
								AND = { # Cannot depose liege when our liege is currently involved in such a war
									attacker = {
										character = PREVPREV
									}
									OR = {
										using_cb = bid_for_independence
										using_cb = depose_liege
									}
								}
								AND = { # Cannot depose liege if someone else is already deposing liege
									defender = {
										character = PREVPREV
									}
									using_cb = depose_liege
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			custom_tooltip = {
				text = TOOLTIPdepose_liegeWARB
				hidden_tooltip = {
					NOT = {
						liege = {
							NOT = { character = PREV }
							OR = {
								is_primary_war_attacker = yes
								is_primary_war_defender = yes
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	can_use = {
		universal_cb_restrictions_excl_NW_KG_trigger = yes
		ROOT = {
			de_facto_liege = FROM
		}
	}

	is_valid = {
		universal_cb_valid_restrictions_trigger = yes
		FROM = {
			any_demesne_title = {
				NOT = { lower_tier_than = ROOT }
				temporary = no
			}
			NOT = { has_character_modifier = installed_pretender } #No longer valid if actual target was replaced by a pretender
		}
	}

	on_add = {
		e_rebels = {
			persistent_event_target:chronicle_player = {
				if = {
					limit = { character = ROOT }
					chronicle = {
						entry = CHRONICLE_WAR_REVOLT_ATTACKER
						portrait = [From.GetID]
					}
					break = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { character = FROM }
					chronicle = {
						entry = CHRONICLE_WAR_REVOLT_DEFENDER
						portrait = [Root.GetID]
					}
					break = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_liege_or_above = ROOT }
					chronicle = {
						entry = CHRONICLE_WAR_REVOLT_ATTACKER_LIEGE
						portrait = [Root.GetID]
					}
					break = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_liege_or_above = FROM }
					chronicle = {
						entry = CHRONICLE_WAR_REVOLT_DEFENDER_LIEGE
						portrait = [From.GetID]
					}
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = { set_character_flag = depose_liege_target } #Mark initial target
	}

	on_success = {
		hidden_tooltip = { ROOT = { add_character_modifier = { name = victory_timer duration = 3 } } }
		FROM = {
			prestige = -500
			change_variable = { which = fear_actions value = -20 }
			war_lost_lose_authority_effect = yes
			if = { #Night's watch versus Night's king, dethrone
				limit = {
					ROOT = { trait = nightswatch }
					has_landed_title = k_nightswatch
				}
				k_nightswatch = { destroy_landed_title = THIS }
				if = {
					limit = { has_landed_title = d_nightswatch }
					d_nightswatch = {
						succession = open_elective
						gender_succ = agnatic
						holder_scope = {
							recalc_succession = yes
							set_government_type = NW_government
							set_global_flag = new_NW_LC_needed
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_landed_title = d_brotherhood
					d_brotherhood = { has_title_flag = brotherhood_rebellion }
				}
				if = {
					limit = { character = 1059 } #Stoneheart
					k_riverlands = {
						if = {
							limit = { holder_scope = { dynasty = 127 } } #Frey
							usurp_title = ROOT
						}
						any_de_jure_vassal_title = {
							limit = {
								holder_scope = { dynasty = 127 }
								NOT = { title = d_thecrossing }
								NOT = { location = { duchy = { title = d_thecrossing } } }
							}
							usurp_title = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = { character = 1303 }
					c_blackhaven = {
						holder_scope = {
							abdicate_to = ROOT
						}
					}
				}
				e_iron_throne = { holder_scope = { ROOT = { set_defacto_liege = PREV } } }
				activate_title = { title = d_brotherhood status = no }
				d_brotherhood = {
					clr_title_flag = brotherhood_rebellion
					destroy_landed_title = THIS
				}
			}
			if = { #Leader choose outcome (abdicate, usurp etc)
				limit = {
					OR = {
						NOT = { has_landed_title = k_the_most_devout }
						ROOT_FROM = { is_merchant_republic = yes }
					}
				}
				custom_tooltip = {
					text = TOOLTIP45370
					ROOT_FROM = {
						save_event_target_as = depose_liege_target
						ROOT = { character_event = { id = 45370 } }
					}
				}
			}
			if = { #High Septon can choose successor
				limit = {
					has_landed_title = k_the_most_devout
					ROOT_FROM = { is_merchant_republic = no }
				}
				character_event = { id = religious.22 tooltip = TOOLTIPreligious.22 }
				hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = maintenance.21 days = 1 } } #Take dejure vassals (AGOT)
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				# If claimant needs a regent, war leader becomes regent if possible
				character_event = { id = regency.55 days = 2 }
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			participation_scaled_prestige = 250
		}
		any_attacker = {
			limit = { NOT = { character = ROOT } }
			hidden_tooltip = { participation_scaled_prestige = 250 }
		}
	}

	on_fail = {
		ROOT = {
			prestige = -100
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_landed_title = d_brotherhood
					d_brotherhood = { has_title_flag = brotherhood_rebellion }
				}
				e_iron_throne = { holder_scope = { ROOT = { set_defacto_liege = PREV } } }
				d_brotherhood = { clr_title_flag = brotherhood_rebellion }
			}
		}
		FROM = { clr_character_flag = depose_liege_target }
	}

	on_reverse_demand = {
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				add_character_modifier = { name = victory_timer duration = 3 }
				change_variable = { which = fear_actions value = 10 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = {
							OR = {
								higher_tier_than = DUKE
								relative_power_including_allies_attacker = { who = PREV power = 0.3 }
							}
						}
					}
					remove_character_modifier = defeated_major_revolt
					add_character_modifier = { name = defeated_major_revolt duration = 3650 }
				}
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			prestige = -200
			prisoner = FROM
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_landed_title = d_brotherhood
					d_brotherhood = { has_title_flag = brotherhood_rebellion }
				}
				hidden_tooltip = {
					any_courtier = {
						limit = {
							prisoner = no
							is_abroad = no
						}
						imprison = FROM
						clr_character_flag = captured_in_battle
					}
					activate_title = { status = no title = d_brotherhood }
				}
				d_brotherhood = {
					clr_title_flag = brotherhood_rebellion
					destroy_landed_title = yes
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			participation_scaled_prestige = 50
		}
		any_defender = {
			limit = { NOT = { character = FROM } }
			hidden_tooltip = { participation_scaled_prestige = 50 }
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			mega_war_emperor_rebels_resolution_effect = yes
		}
		FROM = { clr_character_flag = depose_liege_target }
	}
	on_invalidation = {
		FROM = { clr_character_flag = depose_liege_target }
		ROOT = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_landed_title = d_brotherhood
					d_brotherhood = { has_title_flag = brotherhood_rebellion }
				}
				e_iron_throne = { holder_scope = { ROOT = { set_defacto_liege = PREV } } }
				d_brotherhood = { clr_title_flag = brotherhood_rebellion }
			}
		}
	}

	attacker_ai_victory_worth = {
		factor = -1 # always accept
	}

	attacker_ai_defeat_worth = {
		factor = 150
	}

	defender_ai_victory_worth = {
		factor = -1 # always accept
	}

	defender_ai_defeat_worth = {
		factor = 100
	}

	# ai importance placed on this CB: scope is the targeted title, ROOT is the attacking character, FROM is the defending character
	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 1
		#Dragon intimidation
		modifier = {
			factor = 0
			ROOT = {
				NOT = { can_use_dragon_abilities_trigger = yes }
				NOT = { relative_power = { who = FROM power = 6 } }
			}
			FROM = {
				can_use_dragon_abilities_trigger = yes
				OR = {
					any_friend = { trait = dragon martial = 60 }
					AND = {  graphical_culture = dragongfx martial = 60 }
				}
				is_incapable = no
			}
		}
	}
}
overthrow_ruler = {
	name = CB_NAME_OVERTHROWRULER
	war_name = WAR_NAME_OVERTHROWRULER
	sprite = 12
	truce_days = 3650

	is_revolt_cb = yes
	can_call_vassals = yes
	is_tyranny_cb = yes
	#major_revolt = yes

	infamy_modifier = 0

	can_use = {
		universal_cb_restrictions_excl_NW_KG_trigger = yes
		# ROOT = {
			# de_facto_liege = FROM
		# }
	}

	is_valid = {
		universal_cb_valid_restrictions_trigger = yes
		ROOT = {
			OR = {
				liege = {
					character = PREV # either independent
				}
				liege = {
					FROM = {
						is_liege_or_above = PREV # or have shared liege
					}
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			any_demesne_title = {
				NOT = { lower_tier_than = ROOT }
				temporary = no
			}
			NOT = { has_character_modifier = installed_pretender } #No longer valid if actual target was replaced by a pretender
		}
	}

	on_add = {
		e_rebels = {
			persistent_event_target:chronicle_player = {
				if = {
					limit = { character = ROOT }
					chronicle = {
						entry = CHRONICLE_WAR_REVOLT_ATTACKER
						portrait = [From.GetID]
					}
					break = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { character = FROM }
					chronicle = {
						entry = CHRONICLE_WAR_REVOLT_DEFENDER
						portrait = [Root.GetID]
					}
					break = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_liege_or_above = ROOT }
					chronicle = {
						entry = CHRONICLE_WAR_REVOLT_ATTACKER_LIEGE
						portrait = [Root.GetID]
					}
					break = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { is_liege_or_above = FROM }
					chronicle = {
						entry = CHRONICLE_WAR_REVOLT_DEFENDER_LIEGE
						portrait = [From.GetID]
					}
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			set_character_flag = depose_liege_target
		}
	}

	on_success = {
		hidden_tooltip = { ROOT = { add_character_modifier = { name = victory_timer duration = 3 } } }
		any_attacker = {
			limit = { NOT = { character = ROOT } }
			hidden_tooltip = {
				participation_scaled_prestige = 250
				character_event = { id = mega_wars.12 } #re-vassalise if needed
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			if = { #sub vassal rebellion
				limit = { has_character_flag = sub_vassal_rebellion }
				hidden_tooltip = {
					save_event_target_as = captured_vassal
					FROM = {
						save_event_target_as = enforcer
						if = {
							limit = { has_character_flag = enforce_justice_liege_1 }
							liege = { character_event = { id = 40035 } }
							clr_character_flag = enforce_justice_liege_1
						}
						if = {
							limit = { has_character_flag = enforce_justice_liege_2 }
							liege = { liege = { character_event = { id = 40035 } } }
							clr_character_flag = enforce_justice_liege_2
						}
						if = {
							limit = { has_character_flag = enforce_justice_liege_3 }
							liege = { liege = { liege = { character_event = { id = 40035 } } } }
							clr_character_flag = enforce_justice_liege_3
						}
					}
				}
				clr_character_flag = sub_vassal_rebellion
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			prestige = -500
			change_variable = { which = fear_actions value = -20 }
			remove_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = declared_war
			}
			war_lost_lose_authority_effect = yes
			if = {
				limit = { #Slavers introduce slavery
					ROOT = {
						tier = KING
						OR = {
							has_slavery_religion_trigger = yes
							has_slavery_culture_trigger = yes
							trait = slave_owner
							trait = slave_trader
							culture_group = iron_isles_culture
						}
						NOT = { has_dynasty_flag = liberator_dynasty }
						NOT = { trait = liberator }
						primary_title = {
							OR = {
								has_law = slavery_2
								has_law = slavery_3
							}
						}
					}
				}
				any_demesne_title = { # All titles
					limit = {
						tier = EMPEROR
						NOT = { has_law = slavery_2 }
						NOT = { has_law = slavery_3 }
					}
					if = {
						limit = { ROOT = { primary_title = { has_law = slavery_2 } } }
						add_law = slavery_2
					}
					if = {
						limit = { ROOT = { primary_title = { has_law = slavery_3 } } }
						add_law = slavery_3
					}
				}
			}
			ROOT = {
				show_scope_change = no
				if = { #Leader choose outcome (abdicate, usurp etc)
					limit = {
						OR = {
							NOT = { has_landed_title = k_the_most_devout }
							ROOT_FROM = { is_merchant_republic = yes }
						}
					}
					custom_tooltip = {
						text = TOOLTIP45370
						ROOT_FROM = {
							save_event_target_as = depose_liege_target
							ROOT = { character_event = { id = 45370 } }
						}
					}
				}
				if = { #High Septon can choose successor
					limit = {
						has_landed_title = k_the_most_devout
						ROOT_FROM = { is_merchant_republic = no }
					}
					character_event = { id = religious.22 tooltip = TOOLTIPreligious.22 }
					hidden_tooltip = { character_event = { id = maintenance.21 days = 1 } } #Take dejure vassals (AGOT)
				}
			}
			hidden_tooltip = {
				# If claimant needs a regent, war leader becomes regent if possible
				ROOT = { character_event = { id = regency.55 days = 2 } }
			}
			clr_character_flag = depose_liege_target
		}
		ROOT = {
			participation_scaled_prestige = 250
		}
	}

	on_fail = {
		ROOT = {
			prestige = -100
			if = { #sub vassal rebellion
				limit = { has_character_flag = sub_vassal_rebellion }
				FROM = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_character_flag = enforce_justice_liege_1 }
						liege = { ROOT = { imprison = PREV clr_character_flag = captured_in_battle } }
						clr_character_flag = enforce_justice_liege_1
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_character_flag = enforce_justice_liege_2 }
						liege = { liege = { ROOT = { imprison = PREV clr_character_flag = captured_in_battle } } }
						clr_character_flag = enforce_justice_liege_2
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_character_flag = enforce_justice_liege_3 }
						liege = { liege = { liege = { ROOT = { imprison = PREV clr_character_flag = captured_in_battle } } } }
						clr_character_flag = enforce_justice_liege_3
					}
					save_event_target_as = enforcer
					hidden_tooltip = {
						ROOT = {
							save_event_target_as = captured_vassal
							host = { letter_event = { id = 40032 } }
						}
					}
				}
				clr_character_flag = sub_vassal_rebellion
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			remove_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = declared_war
			}
		}
		FROM = { clr_character_flag = depose_liege_target }
		any_attacker = {
			limit = { NOT = { character = ROOT } }
			hidden_tooltip = {
				character_event = { id = mega_wars.12 } #re-vassalise if needed
			}
		}
	}

	on_reverse_demand = {
		hidden_tooltip = {
			FROM = {
				add_character_modifier = { name = victory_timer duration = 3 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						ROOT = {
							OR = {
								higher_tier_than = DUKE
								relative_power_including_allies_attacker = { who = PREV power = 0.3 }
							}
						}
					}
					change_variable = { which = fear_actions value = 10 }
					remove_character_modifier = defeated_major_revolt
					add_character_modifier = { name = defeated_major_revolt duration = 3650 }
				}
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			prestige = -200
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_character_flag = sub_vassal_rebellion } }
				prisoner = FROM
			}
			if = { #sub vassal rebellion
				limit = { has_character_flag = sub_vassal_rebellion }
				FROM = {
					if = {
						limit = { has_character_flag = enforce_justice_liege_1 }
						liege = { ROOT = { imprison = PREV clr_character_flag = captured_in_battle } }
						clr_character_flag = enforce_justice_liege_1
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_character_flag = enforce_justice_liege_2 }
						liege = { liege = { ROOT = { imprison = PREV clr_character_flag = captured_in_battle } } }
						clr_character_flag = enforce_justice_liege_2
					}
					if = {
						limit = { has_character_flag = enforce_justice_liege_3 }
						liege = { liege = { liege = { ROOT = { imprison = PREV clr_character_flag = captured_in_battle } } } }
						clr_character_flag = enforce_justice_liege_3
					}
					save_event_target_as = enforcer
					hidden_tooltip = {
						ROOT = {
							save_event_target_as = captured_vassal
							host = { letter_event = { id = 40032 } }
						}
					}
				}
				clr_character_flag = sub_vassal_rebellion
			}
			#Hand over any exiles
			if = {
				limit = { FROM = { tier = EMPEROR } }
				any_courtier = {
					limit = {
						is_ruler = no
						liege = { character = PREVPREV }
						any_claim = { tier = EMPEROR holder_scope = { character = FROM } }
						OR = {
							has_character_flag = exiled_royal_family
							reverse_has_opinion_modifier = {
								who = FROM
								modifier = opinion_exiled_pretender
							}
						}
						NOT = { dynasty = FROM }
						NOT = { has_opinion_modifier = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_merciful } }
					}
					hidden_tooltip = {
						move_character = FROM
						if = {
							limit = { trait = slave }
							reverse_remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_my_slave }
							remove_opinion = { who = ROOT modifier = opinion_my_owner }
							reverse_opinion = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_my_slave }
							opinion = { who = FROM modifier = opinion_my_owner }
						}
					}
					imprison = FROM
					clr_character_flag = captured_in_battle
				}
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			participation_scaled_prestige = 50
		}
		any_defender = {
			limit = { NOT = { character = FROM } }
			hidden_tooltip = { participation_scaled_prestige = 50 }
		}
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_attacker = {
				limit = { NOT = { character = ROOT } }
				hidden_tooltip = {
					character_event = { id = mega_wars.12 } #re-vassalise if needed
				}
			}
			any_attacker = {
				limit = { liege = { character = FROM } }
				disband_event_forces = faction_revolters
				add_character_modifier = {
					name = faction_council_power_ultimatum_timer
					hidden = yes
					duration = 3650
				}
			}
			mega_war_emperor_rebels_resolution_effect = yes
		}
		FROM = { clr_character_flag = depose_liege_target }
	}

	on_defender_leader_death = {
		hidden_tooltip = {
			any_attacker = {
				letter_event = {
					id = 251
				}
			}
		}

			if = { #sub vassal rebellion
				limit = { has_character_flag = sub_vassal_rebellion }

						}
						if = {

							clr_character_flag = enforce_justice_liege_2
						}
						if = {
							limit = { has_character_flag = enforce_justice_liege_3 }
							liege = { liege = { liege = { character_event = { id = 40035 } } } }
							clr_character_flag = enforce_justice_liege_3
						}
					}
				}
				clr_character_flag = sub_vassal_rebellion
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			clr_character_flag = depose_liege_target
		}
		any_attacker = {
			limit = { NOT = { character = ROOT } }
			hidden_tooltip = {
				character_event = { id = mega_wars.12 } #re-vassalise if needed
			}
		}
		end_war = invalid
	}
	on_invalidation = {
		ROOT = {
			clr_character_flag = sub_vassal_rebellion
		}
		FROM = {
			clr_character_flag = depose_liege_target
			clr_character_flag = enforce_justice_liege_1
			clr_character_flag = enforce_justice_liege_2
			clr_character_flag = enforce_justice_liege_3
		}
		any_attacker = {
			limit = { NOT = { character = ROOT } }
			hidden_tooltip = {
				character_event = { id = mega_wars.12 } #re-vassalise if needed
			}
		}
	}
